[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark JSON [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector during fuzzing tests. The issue occurs when processing JSON strings with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate pairs, specifically in the `json_string_unescape` function. [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reports a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte READ overflow at address [0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[39m, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccessing memory immediately after a [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte allocated region.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow. The vulnerability allows reading [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone byte beyond the end of an allocated heap buffer.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs during the processing of a JSON input containing Unicode [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate pair escape sequences. The triggering input appears to be a JSON object [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a [0m[32m"surrogates"[0m[39m field containing the value `[0m[32m"\U0000d83d\U0000"[0m[39m`, which [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepresents malformed Unicode surrogate pairs.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace indicates the following call sequence:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m initiates dissection of the input[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The frame dissector processes the packet[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The JSON dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_json`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tvbparse_get`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processes the JSON structure[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The `after_value` callback is executed[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. `get_json_string` is called to extract the string value[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. The overflow occurs in `json_string_unescape` at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m29[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte region that was overflowed was allocated through:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `wmem_strbuf_finalize` at line [0m[1;36m388[0m[39m in wmem_strbuf.c[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Called from `get_json_string` at line [0m[1;36m564[0m[39m in packet-json.c[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocation was performed via `g_realloc` from the GLib library[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs when attempting to read at address [0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[39m, which is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly at the boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m the allocated region [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x50300012dcc0[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Boundary Condition**: The overflow occurs at the exact end of the allocated [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer, suggesting an off-by-one error or incorrect length calculation in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring unescaping logic.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Unicode Handling**: The malformed Unicode surrogate pair in the input [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`\U0000d83d\U0000`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m appears to trigger the issue. The first surrogate [0m[1;39m([0m[39md83d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid high surrogate, but it's followed by an incomplete or malformed low surrogate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequence.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **String Processing**: The issue manifests during the unescape operation, which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocesses escape sequences in JSON strings and converts them to their actual [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacter representations.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Areas for Investigation[0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **epan/dissectors/packet-json.c**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m946[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m1007[0m[39m: The callback execution and parsing framework[0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis matches the pattern used in:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m276[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitial `\U` handling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m326[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m333[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m337[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msurrogate `\u` handling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m425[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m429[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m436[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m440[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitial `\u` handling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix Grammar [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRecommended - Defense in Depth[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `epan/dissectors/packet-json.c` lines [0m[1;36m1310[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1313[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action:** Split the Unicode escape sequence grammar to differentiate between `\u`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `\U` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m1310[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1313[0m[39m with two separate sequences:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. One for `\u` followed by exactly [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. One for `\U` followed by exactly [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange from:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvbparse_set_seq[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvbparse_chars[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[32m"uU"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvbparse_chars[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[32m"0123456789abcdefABCDEF"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvbparse_set_seq[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvbparse_char[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[32m"u"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvbparse_chars[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[32m"0123456789abcdefABCDEF"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvbparse_set_seq[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvbparse_char[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[32m"U"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvbparse_chars[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m[32m"0123456789abcdefABCDEF"[0m[39m, NULL, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis prevents malformed inputs like `\U0000` from being accepted by the parser, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproviding defense in depth.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistency**: The fix applies the same boundary checking pattern used [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the rest of the function, maintaining code consistency and readability.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only adds the missing checks without restructuring existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic, reducing risk of introducing new bugs.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Patch [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m fixes the immediate crash, while Patch [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m prevents [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed input from reaching the vulnerable code path.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Standards Compliance**: Aligns with documented behavior in [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`doc/man_pages/wireshark-filter.adoc` lines [0m[1;36m380[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m381[0m[39m which specify `\uNNNN` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vs `\UNNNNNNNN` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Surrogate Pair Handling**: The fix preserves the existing surrogate pair [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation logic at lines [0m[1;36m370[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m, only adding safety checks.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Unicode Validation**: Existing `IS_TRAIL_SURROGATE` and `SURROGATE_VALUE` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmacro usage remains unchanged.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Output Buffer Management**: No changes to `wmem_strbuf` operations which [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready handle dynamic growth correctly.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Other Escape Sequences**: No impact on handling of `\u`, `\n`, `\t`, `\"`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39metc.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents Buffer Overflow**: Boundary check at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m prevents reading beyond[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`string_length`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Validates Input Characters**: Nibble validation ensures only valid hex [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters are processed.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Graceful Error Handling**: Sets `is_valid_unicode_character = false` and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbreaks, allowing the function to continue processing or skip the invalid sequence.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Grammar Enforcement**: Grammar fix prevents malformed escape sequences from [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing parsed as valid tokens in the first place.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Previously [0m[32m"Accepted"[0m[39m Malformed Input**: Input like `\U0000` will now be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejected or handled as invalid.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is correct behavior per JSON and Unicode standards. [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMalformed input should not be silently accepted.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error Reporting**: Invalid sequences are silently skipped by setting [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`is_valid_unicode_character = false`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This matches existing behavior for other validation failures [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the function. More explicit error reporting could be added later if needed.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Performance**: Additional boundary checks add minimal overhead [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone comparison[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper hex digit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The performance impact is negligible compared to the safety [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbenefit, and matches the overhead already present in other branches.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m276[0m[39m**: Initial `\U` handling already uses this exact pattern[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m326[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m333[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m337[0m[39m**: Surrogate `\u` handling uses this pattern  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m425[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m429[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m436[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m440[0m[39m**: Initial `\u` handling uses this pattern[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **wiretap/netmon.c lines [0m[1;36m285[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m296[0m[39m**: Reference implementation shows proper [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate pair validation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix applies the well-established pattern consistently across all code paths.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
